Tarot cards:  Fool: is a fake and will trick you. High priestess: next player who dies gets revived or revives all the dead players who are already dead. Tower: Ghost interaction. Death: starts a cursed hunt. Hanged man: kills the person who pulled this card. Hermit: freezes the ghost in place for a bit. Devil: Ghost Event. Sun: gives the player who pulled this card full sanity. Moon: drains the players sanity to 0%. Wheel of fortune: has a green and red mist color, Green gives the player 25% sanity, Red drains 25% sanity from the player.

Some helpful tips for this new version are:  Turn off your light, and don't speak when the ghost is hunting.  If you say "I'm scared" or "I'm so scared, the ghost will become more active, similar to when you say the name of the ghost.  Doors can sometimes be used as hiding places if angled properly  The Tarot Cards have a chance of reviving a dead teammate, or can be used as an extra life if drawn before the death of said teammate.  Yokai are very sensitive to noise, do not say it's name when around the ghost room of a Yokai.  The mirror breaks (I think) if it does a full rotation of the room and sees itself  Pick up the car keys (if there is a car) and click on the car to stop the honking   Fingerprints can be found on windows, door, and light switches.  You can place a recording camera on the tripod so you don't take up an extra item slot, but do that last so you can pick up your other 2 items.  The Crucifix does not stop cursed hunts, so do not put that on a summoning circle, it's not going to do anything.  Using the radio during a hunt will make the ghost even more aggressive.  Some ghosts revolve around the status of the fuse box, such as the Jinn.   Dirty water doesn't do anything, it just kinda exists. It might be able to give an objective sometimes, I don't remember.   D.O.T.S can be placed on the wall and floor and it's for seeing an image of the ghost walking around. The Goryo will not appear on D.O.T.S if you are in the room. (Not sure if it is also the house)  Freezing temperatures are sometimes only a sign of a ghost event, and do not count as evidence in that case.  If you see a six fingered handprint, it is either an Obake or a Mimic copying the Obake.  You can change the thermometer from Celsius to Fahrenheit in settings.  The "Escape a ghost during a hunt" objective is rarely worth the risk.  Take pictures of fingerprints, bones, interactions, journal writing, salt footprints, UV footprints (not evidence) for some extra money.   Wraiths hover above the ground, but if they touch salt, they immediately disappear unless it's during a hunt (I think)  The Fool means that whatever effect the tarot cards had, is not true and you've been pranked pet say.  Personally, I do not think head cameras are worth the expense, but that's just in my experience.  Do not use the Ouija Board if you are low on sanity, this will trigger a cursed hunt. Also, if you say hide and seek to it, RUN. Remember to say goodbye when you are done with the Ouija board, or it will explode, and that will also trigger a cursed hunt.   The voodoo doll does not have a 100% chance of starting a hunt, but if the heart pin is touched, hide as fast as you can.  If you crouch under the motion sensor, it will not detect you.  Hope this helps you and anyone else who reads this!
